They finished the entire work within one day, and provided drywall repair for me the day after to patch up the minor drywall imperfections incurred by the installation.

Overall, Swift Water Heater is a professional, dedicated and "swift" company, managed by a responsible and responsive owner, Jay. I would recommend Swift Water Heater to people I know for water heater installations or other plumbing requests.

Thank you Jay for the good work of you and your team!

Bowen< /text>

<Text>Update:

After discovering that Nelson's technician made the mistake on using an used 70 amp breaker vs. a 20 on my home, another technician came out and fixed it very promptly.

I understand that businesses should have a markup, it's cost of doing business but that's still a 20x markup. <Rating>1</Rating><userid>116518361529002725521<//userid><username>Hector de los Santos<//username>< Review>
Well I wished this is one of those you-get-what-you-paid-for kind of review. Spoiler alert! It is NOT.

Brief Summary: I was given an estimate of $106/hr for approx. 7 hours worth of job thinking it would probably rack up to about $850-900 total considering some wiggle room with adjustments and materials. I Ended getting billed for $1485 after the job is complete without any sort of heads up prior and during the process. You are better off looking elsewhere to take your business to.

Here's the story. I need help with a few electrical tasks on my house such as installing exterior lights, ceiling fans, etc. Went to yelp, asked around for estimates from a few companies. Nelson responded really quicklu and gave a really good estimate that's hard to pass on. $106 per hour for approx 7 hour job, do the math. I signed up with them thinking I could save a couple of hundred dollars and I was dead wrong! The estimate was just for labor even after I've given them a very very detailed description of what I need done. They did mention that in there long disclaimer that I obviously missed. To my defense all the estimates I recieved for this job are with materials included so I just did not think this would be any different at the time. LESSON LEARNED. A VERY EXPENSIVE LESSON that is. Here's the catch, they get you by grossly overcharging for their materials without any warnings or form of communication prior or during the job. I called them about it and all I got was "it was in the disclaimer" that they can (oh and they will) slap you with a whopping amount of $$$ on materials after the job is complete. These are things you can get from HomeDepot for a third of the price if not less.

Here's my review of the actual electricians that worked on my house.

Pros:
Alex and Benicio (the guys that worked on my house) came wearing masks.
They were always on time and friendly.
The electrical job Benicio worked on works.
I'm sure these 2 guys are good people that work for a scammy people.

Cons:
They say the job includes a "light" patch job (again, in their disclaimer). But I prefer they just didn't even try to patch. Please see pictures.
Lack of communication skills. Some things had to be re-done because they weren't done properly.
They did not clean up. Left everything dirty and did not even dispose things and materials they used. I had to clean up after them a lot and dispose the used ceiling fans myself.
No sense of "final touches" by leaving outlets open and not providing proper wall plates. I would be okay with this if I'm getting some kind of savings but this is definitely not the case.

Conclusion

I will never work nor will ever recommend this company even to my enemies. My hope of trying to save some $$$ ended being the most expensive choice I made. Other companies actually did quote me for around $1100 with everything included, no-surprises, no-disclaimer, no-fineprint BS. But I ended with $1500 for a service that is definitely not worth that. Just look at the pictures.<//Review>

<rate>4<//rate>< review>
My Fiance and I needed a few updates to our home so we sought Omega Electrical help and expertise. Our point guy was Nelson, completely satisfied for two thirds of the projects but we feel the crew handling the other 3rd could of been more professional.

Electrical Box:
The work came out amazing. It took them a bit longer to finish then they projected but the results were amazing.  They estimated about 8 hours of work  but it took them close to 12 hours. Nelson kindly communicated the reason for the delay, the new electrical box was not fitting correctly to the wall. We had electricity power running to the house by the end of the day. For any person interested in updating their electrical box, double check that the number of neutral wires is equal to the number of hot wires. In our case 1 neutral was used between 2 hot wires and it was not caught during the upgrade of the panel. This did not pass first inspection (ask your point person at the end of the project). Nelson was kindly enough to fix the issue later although we felt they should of know better if they're following all electrical codes. It took 3 times for the inspector to pass the project. Nelson and Omega Electrical crew came ahead of time every day to meet and greet the inspector. They were friendly enough so we let them into our home without us being there (3 separate days). First inspector Visit - the neutral and hot wire count did not match - this is not normal and the inspector asked them to fix it, along with adding a metal flange. 2nd Inspector Visit  - Wrong Screws were used on the electrical box (Easy Fix ). 3rd Inspector Visit - Passed with flying colors. I'm posting this for any reader interested in saving themselves time. As the inspector had to show up on 3 different days.

20amp Outlet to Garage Office:
This was done on day 1 of the project and came out great. The location is a bit awkward for the outlet but the Omega Electrical crew let us know why it was placed in the awkward location. Not a big deal but I wish they would have told us the location before hand.

Exterior Level 2 Car Charge:
Ok this is where things got rocky with them. Car Charger was installed on the following visit - Day 2. By this time  of project had been completed and Omega Electrical had been paid for the previous project. We only saw Nelson at the beginning of the day and I think that is where things fell apart. The crew that day was not as neat and professional as the crew from Day 1. Inside the house they left all sorts of random materials and debris. The pipe leading into the exterior outlet was bent (seems like it wasn't a perfect fit, so the electrical pipe looks like it was forced into place). On day 1 of the projects I saw Nelson come by and attend his crew with water and coffee, clean up any random debri left on the ground ( he legit brought a wireless vacuum to pick up stuff). What we saw on Day 2 was different. The hallway necessary to access the electrical cable line had been previously painted. This wall was left filty with hand prints and scratches by ladders. My home is in the process of being updated so fair warning to any homeowner that has their finish look in place. Day 2 crew was not as clean. Does the car charger work? Yes. Sadly my fiance and I will be repainting the hallways again.

Hope this is a fair review and only want to describe/point out my experience. Omega Electrical prices are fair and I wish them all the best. I would definitely use them for my future grounding electrical work, and will personally ask for Nelson to help us.<//review>

< Text>
During summer 2020, our 5yo was missing social interaction and needing activities. We were so blessed to find summer camp at Safari Run. Even though he was the youngest at camp and we as parents were worries, the staff did a fantastic job of relieving our worries and of making him feel a part of the group. When his birthday was coming up this fall, we booked a private play session for him and a few friends. He's been talking about Safari Camp and the "big structure" for months, so it was a real treat to get to go back and show everything to his friends. They had a *blast* exploring and having the entire place to themselves. The staff were welcoming and inviting, and made us all feel very comfortable in terms of health/safety protocols. An extra plus, they remembered Rohan from summer camp and made him feel extra special!< /Text>

Cost wise I think I overpaid for the amount of food and the quality of it as well. $20+ for 6 tacos and a torta seemed a bit much.

The torta I got for my wife and it looked quite good and ample size. She didn‚Äôt have any complaints over it.

I got 4 asada and 2 carnitas. The carnita tacos were plain with diced tomato. It really took away from the flavor of the meat and almost tarnished it. The asada tacos had the normal taco fare on top of it, but still not much flavor. They give you a choice of green and red salsa, but neither was spicy and was more bland, maybe to tailor to the a American clients nearby.

The only reason I went was because I‚Äôve been to the original one in Woodlake and I had a Restaurant dot com certificate. Unfortunately I don‚Äôt think I will go back for a while.</review>

We were at the Riverway Sports Complex and a friend of ours recommended this place. I have the carne asada burrito, my wife had a burrito with buche and carnitas. My son had the chili verde burrito and my other son had two tacos (1 barbacoa and 1 pollo). It all was very good. My carne asada burrito was great, it had no chewy bits of asada.
